Appendix H - Ayahuasca Study Participant Information Sheet

Participant Information Sheet

PARTICIPANT INFORMATION SHEET
[A Study on the Phenomenology and Psychological Outcomes of Ritualistic Ayahuasca
Induced Experiences in Peru.]

You are being invited to take part in a research project. Before you decide whether you
want to take part, it is important for you to understand why the research is being done
and what will be involved. Please take the time to read the following information carefully.

Who is conducting the research?

The project is being conducted by Ross Bartlett, as part of his research degree in
psychology at Buckinghamshire New University.

What is the purpose of the study?

This study will investigate the happenings and mental outcomes of ayahuasca induced
experiences. It is hoped that the findings of this study will contribute to the existing
body of knowledge and, perhaps, be of help to people looking to find answers on their
own experiences. Further, it should help add to the understanding of the potential
therapeutic use of ayahuasca.

What is involved in participating?

You will be asked to answer a number of questions. There are no right or wrong
answers and it is not a test. The questions will simply explore your experiences and
possible psychological outcomes. In order to participate, it is required that you have a
reasonable ability to read and speak English conversationally. All interviews will be
conducted one on one and will be in a location within public view, but not within a
distance that people could listen in on the interview. It is important that the information
remains private.

Will what I say or do in this study be kept confidential?

You will not be asked to give your name or any identification during the interview, and
all the information you give will be confidential. On the participant consent form you
will be able to indicate a desired pseudonym for the study. Only the researcher and his
supervisors will have access to the data, which will be stored by the researcher in
accordance with the Buckinghamshire New University policy on data security.

The interview will be recoded onto a digital voice recorder, transcribed and stored on a
password-protected computer. The interview recording will then be deleted and
raw transcribed data will be analysed. The resulting analysed data files will also be
stored on a password-protected computer.

The anonymised data will be used for a thesis and may form part of a published article
and/or conference/seminar paper. The data generated in the course of the research will
be destroyed once the thesis has been examined, or if the data is likely to be used for a
publication and/or conference/seminar paper, it will be transferred to a supervisor and
kept for a period of ten years after the completion of the research project.

NATURE & IMPACT OF OUT-OF-BODY EXPERIENCES

510

Do I have to take part in the study?

No, it is up to you to decide whether to take part, as participation is entirely voluntary. If
you do decide to take part you will be asked to indicate that you have read this sheet and
give consent to take part. Further, you will then be asked to sign a second consent form
just prior to the interview. You are still free to withdraw at any time, up to four weeks
after completing the interview, without giving a reason and without penalty. To do this,
you can email the researcher or phone or write to the psychology department and state
your pseudonym and that you wish to withdraw from the study.

What are the possible benefits and risks of taking part?

Benefits  of  taking  part  in  this  study  include  aiding  research  into  the  understanding  of
ayahuasca and our understanding of the mind. The main beneficiary of the study is the
researcher,  who  will  use  the  data  for  his  research  degree  programme.  No  risks  are
anticipated in taking part in this study.

Can you make an informed decision?

Due  to  your  recent  consumption  of  N,N-Dimethyltryptamine  (DMT)  derived  from  the
shrub, Psychotria viridis, you should be aware that in signing the second consent form
just prior to the interview, you are indicating that you believe you are  able to make an
informed decision on taking part in this study without an impairment of, or a disturbance
in  the  functioning  of,  the  mind  or  brain  even  if  the  nature  of  this  impairment  or
disturbance is temporary.

Who has reviewed the study?

The Research and Ethics Committee at Buckinghamshire New University have approved
this study.

If you have any questions regarding this study, please contact either:

Researcher: Ross Bartlett
Email: ross.bartlett@bucks.ac.uk

Supervisor: Dr Matthew Smith
Email: matthew.smith@bucks.ac.uk

Supervisor: Dr Ciaran O’Keeffe
Email: Ciaran.okeeffe@bucks.ac.uk

Supervisor: Dr Piers Worth
Email: piers.worth@bucks.ac.uk

Department of Psychology
Buckinghamshire New University
Queen Alexandra Road
High Wycombe
Buckinghamshire HP11 2JZ
Tel.: 01494 522 141

Please keep this for your reference.

NATURE & IMPACT OF OUT-OF-BODY EXPERIENCES

511

I understand that my participation is voluntary and understand that I
can refuse to answer questions and I can withdraw from the study at
any time, without having to give a reason. I can withdraw my data
from the study up to four weeks after completing the interview,
without giving reason and without penalty.

I agree to take part in the above study.

I consent to the processing of my personal information for the
purposes of this research study. I understand that such information
will be treated as strictly confidential and handled in accordance
with current UK Data Protection legislation.

has been anonymised) in a specialist data centre and may be used
for future research; and that any researcher who has access to
these data may only do so if they agree to preserve the
confidentiality of these data.

I agree to the interview being audio recorded.

I agree to the use of anonymised quotes in publications.

Appendix J - Ayahuasca Study Debrief Sheet

Debrief Sheet

[A Study on the Phenomenology and Psychological Outcomes of Recent Ayahuasca
Induced Experiences in Peru.]

Thank you very much for taking the time to participate in this study. The purpose of this
study  was  to  gain  a  greater  understanding  of  the  nature  and  psychological  effects  of
ayahuasca induced experiences. For example, it is known that out-of-body experiences
(OBEs) can change an individual’s fear of death, view of self, and lifestyle but the various
mechanisms of these changes are not clear. It is hoped that the findings of this study will
contribute to the existing body of knowledge and, perhaps, be of help to people looking to
find  answers  on  their  own  experiences.  Further,  it  should  help  raise  awareness  of  the
potential therapeutic use of ayahuasca. We hope that you have found it interesting and
have not been upset by any of the topics discussed. However, if you have found any part
of this experience to be distressing or have any further questions you can speak to the
researcher or one of the supervisors via the information below.

Researcher: Ross Bartlett
Email: ross.bartlett@bucks.ac.uk

Supervisor: Dr Matthew Smith
Email: matthew.smith@bucks.ac.uk

Supervisor: Dr Ciaran O’Keeffe
Email: ciaran.okeeffe@bucks.ac.uk

Supervisor: Dr Piers Worth
Email: piers.worth@bucks.ac.uk

Department of Psychology
Buckinghamshire New University
Queen Alexandra Road
High Wycombe
Buckinghamshire HP11 2JZ
Tel.: 01494 522 141

There are also a number of organisations listed below that you can contact.

Appendix K – Paul Interview Transcript

RB: Paul interview

RB: LETS START WITH PARTICIPANT INFORMATION. COULD YOU PLEASE
CONFIRM YOUR GENDER?

P: MALE.

RB: YOUR AGE?

P: 18.

RB: OCCUPATION?

P: FURNITURE SALESMAN.

RB: ANY RELIGIOUS BACKGROUND?

P: NO.

RB: AND HOW MANY TIMES HAVE YOU CONSUMED AYAHUASCA?

P: 3.

RB: CAN WE BRANCH OUT FROM THERE AND YOU CAN TELL ME YOUR MOST
PROFOUND EXPERIENCE, DEPENDING ON HOW YOU FORMULATE
EXPERIENCES, MIGHT BE DIFFICULT TO PICK ONE. JUST START FROM
SOMEWHERE AND WE CAN BRANCH OUT FROM THERE?

P: WELL, I DID THE THREE EXPERIENCES, ONE AND AN OFF DAY, ONE AND AN
OFF DAY, THEN ANOTHER. I THINK THE FIRST ONE WAS MOST PROFOUND
AND THE THIRD ONE I WOULD SAY, BUT THE FIRST ONE I WOULD SAY
SUBJECTIVELY BECAUSE IT WAS THE FIRST TIME I HAD THAT EXPERIENCE, A
BIG LEAP, SO I WOULD SAY IT WAS THE FIRST ONE.

RB: WITH THE FIRST ONE COULD YOU TELL ME HOW THE EXPERIENCE
STARTED?

P: IT WAS A GOOD CENTRE THAT I FOUND, I THINK ON THE FIRST SESSION
THERE WERE NOT MANY OF US. WITH PEOPLES FIRST TIME THEY TEND TO
WANT SMALLER GROUPS BECAUSE THEY CAN BE DIFFICULT TO WORK WITH.
SO THERE WAS SIX OR SEVEN OF US AND THE SHAMAN, THE DOCTOR A
CARDIOLOGIST AND PEOPLE LIKE THAT AND WE WERE GIVEN A CERTAIN
AMOUNT BASED ON THE PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILING DONE ON US TO
DETERMINE THE RISK FACTOR AND I WAS GIVEN ABOUT HALF A CUP. IT
TASTED AWFUL, ONE OF THE WORST THINGS I HAVE EVER TASTED. IT TOOK
QUITE A LONG TIME BEFORE IT HAD ANY EFFECT. WE WERE IN THIS
OUTDOOR HUT AND IT WAS QUITE WARM AND WE WERE IN SLEEPING BAGS

AND LOTS OF BLANKETS. I WAS SAT THERE IN A MEDITATIVE STATE, DOING
THE BEST TO CONCENTRATE ON MY BREATHING, THE STANDARD APPROACH
WHEN PEOPLE WOULD GO INTO IT, THEN WHAT THEY SAID THE FOLLOWING
DAY WAS ABOUT AN HOUR AND A HALF. I THINK I WAS ONE OF THE LAST
PEOPLE TO START FEELING THE EFFECT. I WAS IN A RAIN FOREST, I WASN’T
SURE IF IT WAS JUST IN MY HEAD, ALL MY EARS JUST PICKING UP THE SOUNDS
ALL AROUND. WE WERE IN THE SACRED VALLEY IN PERU, SO THERE WAS A
LOT OF THINGS THAT COULD BE MAKING THAT NOISE LIKE DOGS BARKING.
YOU COULD HEAR BIRDS AND NOISES LIKE THAT, LIKE A HUM LOUDER AND
LOUDER LIKE A HIGH PITCH, LIKE A DOG WHISTLE THAT I HADN’T HEARD
BEFORE. THAT WAS THE FIRST THING THAT I FELT IT WENT ON LONGER AND
LONGER BUT IT PROBABLY DIDN’T. THEN I STARTED TO SEE AND I HAD MY
EYES OPEN AND I HEARD THE NOISE AGAIN. IT WAS VERY DARK AND ALL YOU
COULD SEE WAS THE FIRE AND THE SHAMAN WAS SINGING IN THE CENTRE
AND MOVING ALONG TO EACH PERSON. HE HAD BEEN SINGING SO LONG THAT
I WAS BLOCKING IT OUT OR GOT USED TO IT. ALL I COULD SEE WERE SOME
SHADOWS, THE SHAMAN’S FACE IN THE FIRE AND A LITTLE OPENING IN THE
HUT WE WERE IN WHERE I COULD SEE THE SKY WHICH WAS LIGHTER THAN
IN THE HUT WE WERE IN. THEN I STARTED TO SEE ON TOP OF THAT MULTI
COLOURED DOTS, RED, YELLOW AND OTHER COLOURS PULSING LIKE STATIC
ON THE TELEVISION.

RB: IS THIS WITH YOUR EYES OPEN?

P: YES, WITH MY EYES OPEN, THEN I WAS A LITTLE CONFUSED AS TO
WHETHER THEY WERE OPEN OR SHUT, SO I OPENED THEM AND THEN WHEN I
SHUT THEM IT CAME A LOT MORE VIVID, IT TOOK OVER THE ENTIRE
PERIPHERAL VISION AND THEY KEPT GROWING AND THE NOISE WAS
GETTING LOUDER. IT WASN’T LIKE THREATENING OR SCARY BUT IT WAS
GETTING LOUDER AND THEN I OPENED MY EYES AND IT SUBSIDED A BIT.
SOMETHING THAT WASN’T PHYSICALLY THERE BUT I COULD SEE IT WITH MY
EYES OPEN. THAT’S WHEN I FELT I WAS IN PSYCHEDELIC STATE THAT WAS
BEYOND MY CONTROL. INTERNALLY AT LEAST I DIDN’T FEEL I WAS IN ANY
DANGER BUT EXTERNALLY I FELT I WAS GETTING A BIT MORE LIKE THAT, MY
BODY WAS REACTING EVEN THOUGH MY BRAIN WAS SAYING IT’S KIND OF
FINE, MY BODY WAS SHAKING, I WAS SHAKING QUITE A LOT AND ONE OF THE
NURSES ADVISED THAT I LAY DOWN IN THE SLEEPING BAG AND CLOSED MY
EYES AND THEN IT REALLY STARTED TO TAKE OVER. I FELT FULLY DETACHED
FROM MY BODY AND THE COLOURS BECAME MORE AND MORE VIVID AND
THEY BECAME SHAPES AND THEN THEY BECAME THESE ENTITIES THAT I
HEARD PEOPLE SAY THAT AYAHUASCA CAN DO THIS. THESE ENTITIES, I
THINK, ARE CALLED CLOCKWORK ELVES OR GHOSTS OR ALIENS OR
WHATEVER YOUR INTERPRETATIONS OF THEM ARE. THEY WEREN’T ANY
PARTICULAR FORM, THEY WERE JUST PULSING IN AND OUT OF A SPIRALLY
FRACTAL BACKGROUND, SO NOTHING WAS MATERIALISED AT ANY
PARTICULAR TIME, THEY WERE JUST SHAPES, YOU COULD JUST ENVISAGE A
HUMANOID SHAPE LIKE AN EYE, MAYBE A MOUTH, THEY WERE BECOMING
MORE AND MORE VIVID, I COULD SEE THEM ALL AROUND ME LIKE 360
DEGREES. I COULD TELL THEY WERE COMMUNICATING WITH EACH OTHER

BUT IT WASN’T VERBAL, LIKE IN A LANGUAGE IT WAS TELEPATHIC LIKE AN
INSTANT LANGUAGE. I COULD TELL THEY WERE TALKING ABOUT ME SAYING
HE IS NOT READY TO BE HIT YET, IT’S NOT HIS REALITY YET. I FELT I DIDN’T
HAVE A SAY IN IT. I FELT HELPLESS LIKE AN OBJECT, WHAT SHALL WE DO
WITH THIS THING, THEY WEREN’T BEING HOSTILE. IT WAS UNEMOTIONAL,
WE DON’T NEED HIM. I HAD AN IDEA OF THEM PICKING ME UP AND
THROWING ME AWAY AND I REALISED I HAD SPENT QUITE A LOT OF TIME
NOT IN MY BODY. I DIDN’T KNOW WHERE I WAS, I COULDN’T FEEL MY HANDS,
MY PHYSICAL BODY WAS NOWHERE TO BE FOUND. IT SNUCK UP ON ME I
DIDN’T KNOW AT WHICH POINT I LEFT MY BODY AT THE POINT OF THEM
THROWING ME I REALISED I HAD LEFT MY BODY AND HANG ON HOW LONG
HAD I BEEN IN THIS PLACE AND MY WHOLE PERCEPTION COMPLETELY WENT
OUT THE WINDOW AND I DIDN’T KNOW HOW LONG I HAD BEEN THERE. IT
WAS SCARY BUT A BIT COOL BUT I STILL HAD IT IN MY HEAD THAT I WAS IN
PERU DOING AYAHUASCA DOING THIS EXPERIENCE, I HAD NO IDEA WHERE I
WAS OR WHO I WAS BUT I KNEW I HAD BEEN THROWN AND IT WAS LIKE
TRAVELLING THROUGH LIGHT YEARS, DIFFERENT KINDS OF SPACE AND I WAS
ON THIS JOURNEY, I WAS SEEING TWO THINGS AT ONCE, I WAS SEEING
WHERE I WAS GOING, I WAS LIKE A BEAM OF LIGHT, I WAS IMMATERIAL, I
WAS BEING THROWN INTO DIFFERENT REALITIES NOT ALIENS ON
DIFFERENT PLANETS. IT WAS HARD TO EXPLAIN WITH HUMAN WORDS BUT
DIFFERENT REALITIES. SHAPES THAT WE CAN’T PERCEIVE, I FELT LIKE WHAT
PEOPLE CALL FOUR DIMENSIONAL, SHAPES THAT WOULD NOT EXIST IN OUR
THREE DIMENSIONAL UNIVERSE, SEEING LOADS OF COLOURS THAT I HAD
NOT SEEN BEFORE, DIFFERENT TO THE SPECTRUM THAT DOES EXIST AND AS
I WAS GOING THROUGH I COULD SEE MY OWN LIFE, I COULD EXPERIENCE MY
WHOLE LIFE IN REAL TIME AND AS I CAUGHT UP TO THAT TIME THEN THE
WHOLE THING FLASHED AS IF I HAD BEEN THERE FIVE MINUTES, BUT AT THE
TIME OF EXPERIENCING IT, IT FELT LIKE REAL TIME, IT BECAME WARPED
AND TIME WENT COMPLETELY OUT THE WINDOW. THE SEQUENCE OF THESE
EVENTS MIGHT NOT BE TOO ACCURATE BECAUSE I JUMPED FROM ONE TO
ANOTHER BECAUSE I WAS GOING BACKWARDS AND FORWARDS BUT IT WAS
ALL SIMULTANEOUS AND WHILE THIS WAS HAPPENING AS I WAS FLYING
THROUGH THESE DIMENSIONS I WAS ABLE TO SEE IN THE DISTANCE BEHIND
EVERYTHING WHICH WAS TWO DIMENSIONAL LAYERS AND I WAS ABLE TO
SEE WHERE I PHYSICALLY WAS, I COULD SEE IT FROM ABOVE BUT NOT AS A
POINT OF VIEW. I WAS SHAKING AND CONVULSING AND THROWING MY ARMS
AROUND.

RB: SO, YOU TALKED ABOUT SEEING DIFFERENT THINGS, WERE YOU AT ANY
POINT ABLE TO LOOK BACK AT YOUR PHYSICAL BODY.

P: MY OWN PHYSICAL BODY WHEN I WAS LOOKING AT IT LOOKED VERY
NORMAL, BASIC AND LIKE REAL LIFE. SO THE STATE THAT I WAS IN LOOKING
AT MY MATERIAL SELF AT THE SAME TIME WAS UNINTERESTING.

RB: YOU WERE SEEING THAT FROM A DETACHED PERSPECTIVE?

P: YES. I WAS LOOKING AT MYSELF, THE VERSION I COULD SEE WAS FLINGING

AROUND, I FELT I WAS GOING TO BE SICK BUT I WAS LAUGHING, I KNEW I WAS
GOING TO BE ALRIGHT. BUT IN A WAY IF HE DIES I KNOW THAT IS GOING TO
BE ME. BUT I WAS FINE IT DIDN’T FEEL VERY SIGNIFICANT. THE NEXT DAY
WHEN I SAW EVERYONE I HAD BEEN TAKEN ME TO AN ON-SITE HOSPITAL. IT
TOOK ABOUT THREE PEOPLE TO PICK ME UP BECAUSE I WAS FIGHTING THEM
OFF, TRYING TO STAND UP AND THEN I FELL ONTO SOMEONE ELSE, I WAS
JUST MAKING A NOISE AND BEING DISRUPTIVE. I WALKED INTO THIS
HOSPITAL AND THEY GAVE ME MORPHINE AND THAT CALMED ME DOWN. I
DO HAVE A MEMORY OF THE AYAHUASCA WEARING OFF. I DON’T KNOW IF
THAT WAS THE RESULT OF THE MORPHINE BUT IT WAS JUST SILLY STUFF
AND I WAS TALKING ABOUT POP CULTURE, I WAS TALKING ABOUT MICHAEL
JACKSON. ALL THE NURSES ONLY SPOKE SPANISH AND I DON’T, BUT I WAS
TRYING TO GET THEIR ATTENTION BUT NOBODY WOULD ANSWER ME I WAS
LYING ON THE BED WITH PILES OF BLANKETS AND I WAS BITING THEM, THEN
I SAID MICHAEL JACKSON AND THE PERUVIAN NURSE UNDERSTOOD THAT
AND WAS LAUGHING, I THINK IT WAS THE MORPHINE.

RB: DURING THE TIME OF GOING FROM THE CEREMONY TO THE HOSPITAL, DO
YOU HAVE ANY RECOLLECTION OR AWARENESS OF THAT?

P: YES. MOMENTS OF IT. THE WHOLE SEQUENCE OF THAT EVENING PLAYED
OUT A FEW TIMES FROM DIFFERENT PERSPECTIVES , SO I DO HAVE A VAGUE
RECOLLECTION OF THE WHOLE THING, BUT BIG CHUNKS OF IT ARE NOT
THERE. THAT WAS WHEN I HAD NO ATTENTION ON IT, IT WAS ALL INWARD
BUT I DO JUST REMEMBER FEELING VERY HEAVY AND VERY ODD. I CAN WALK,
IT WILL BE FINE. NOT HAVING ANY EXPERIENCE BEFORE WITH MY MOTOR
FUNCTION WAS REALLY IMPACTED AS MUCH AS THE AYAHUASCA, MUCH
MORE SEVERE THAN OTHER EXPERIENCES FROM SUBSTANCES. I WAS BARELY
ABLE TO STAND, MY LEGS FELT LIKE JELLY AND KEPT COLLAPSING AND
EVENTUALLY THEY HAD ENOUGH PEOPLE TO PICK ME UP AND WALK ME
THROUGH. GOING OUTSIDE FELT REALLY REFRESHING AND I WAS TOUCHING
MY FACE, LOOKING AT MY HANDS, REAL PSYCHEDELIC STUFF, MY SENSES
WERE OVERWHELMED WITH STUFF, LIKE HEARING, SENSES AND SMELLS.
THE ONLY PART BEING SICK FOR THE FIRST TIME I REALLY CAN’T PLACE, THE
SECOND AND THIRD TIME, I CAN. WHERE IN THE SEQUENCE I WAS SICK BUT I
KNEW I COULDN’T FIND THE BUCKET. I HAVE NO RECOLLECTION BUT I HAVE
THE RECOLLECTION OF BEING SICK. I MADE QUITE A MESS AND THEY HAD TO
CLEAN IT AND I FELT QUITE EMBARRASSED THE NEXT DAY. EARLY IN THE
MORNING I HAD NO RECOLLECTION BUT AS THE DAY WENT ON IT CAME
BACK, BEING SICK YOUR SENSES ARE INTENSIFIED IT FELT SO REAL I WASN’T
LOOKING AT ANYTHING. IT FELT LIKE THERE WAS A DEGREE OF HAVING TO
LET GO IN THE BEING SICK THE FIRST TIME, I REALLY DIDN’T FEEL I
ACHIEVED MUCH I DIDN’T DO MUCH WORK, THE EMPHASIS WERE IN THIS
RETREAT ABOUT DOING SOME WORK, IMPROVEMENT AND INTENTIONS BUT I
FELT MY FIRST TIME IT WAS WILD AND I JUMPED STRAIGHT INTO THE DEEP
END, THERE WASN’T MUCH WORK DONE, IT WAS LIKE A SPECTACLE. THE
SECOND ONE WAS NOT SO INTENSE BUT THE THIRD ONE WHEN I WAS BEING
SICK, I JUST REMEMBER SEEING DIFFERENT MOMENTS FROM MY LIFE,
DIFFERENT UNIVERSES I MIGHT HAVE SEEN STUFF THAT WAS ON EARTH,

THINGS IN THE PAST OR THE FUTURE, IT ALL FELT INSIGNIFICANT IN THE
HUGE WEB OF EVERYTHING. IT WAS SO MINUTE BECAUSE THERE WAS BIGGER
STUFF.

RB: THAT’S GREAT STUFF, VERY VIVID. WE WILL MOVE ON TO QUESTIONS
FROM THAT. DO YOU FEEL THAT YOUR EXPERIENCE HAS CHANGED YOUR
VIEW IN ANY WAY OF THE DIVINE?

P: YES, IT HAS. I DON’T COME FROM A RELIGIOUS BACKGROUND, I WOULD SAY
THAT I BELIEVE IN GOD BUT I DON’T KNOW WHAT GOD IS, I THINK IT IS A
SUBJECTIVE THING A FLUID THING. DIFFERENT THINGS AT DIFFERENT TIMES.
THERE IS ALL DIFFERENT THINGS IN MY EYES THAT ARE THE SAME. SO I
BELIEVED IN MY LIFE DIFFERENT CIRCUMSTANCES, LIKE MEDITATION AND I
JUST FELT CONNECTED TO IT. I FELT THERE IS SOMETHING BEYOND,
SOMETHING HUGE THAT WE ARE UNABLE TO PERCEIVE. SO I DID BELIEVE
THAT GOING IN, SO I DID HAVE AN OPEN MIND GOING IN, SO I DO FEEL IN A
SENSE THAT THERE ARE MORE QUESTIONS THAN ANSWERS, BUT IT HAS
DEEPENED MY BELIEF. IT HAS MAYBE ENFORCED MY BELIEFS BUT THERE
WAS A LOT OF THINGS ON DEATH AND REBIRTH AND THAT REINFORCED TO
ME THAT THERE WAS AN AFTERLIFE, BUT WHICH I HADN’T BEEN SURE
ABOUT BEFORE, BUT WITHOUT A SHADOW OF DOUBT THERE IS SOMETHING
MORE THAN WHAT WE KNOW.

RB: WAS THERE ANYTHING SPECIFICALLY ABOUT THE EXPERIENCE, PERHAPS
SEEING SOMETHING, HEARING SOMETHING OR COMING OUT OF YOUR BODY
THAT YOU FEEL TOWARDS THE DEEPENING OR THE EXPANSION OF YOUR
RELATIONSHIP WITH THE DIVINE?

P: ONE PART OF IT INVOLVED ME DYING, I DO IN A SENSE FEEL THAT
HAPPENED, MY HEART PHYSICALLY STOPPED IN THIS INCARNATION ON A
BIOLOGICAL LEVEL BUT I FELT IN A SPIRITUAL LEVEL I HAD DIED IN PART OF
IT AND FOR A WHILE I WAS IN THIS STATE OF NOTHING. IT WAS OK, I WAS
ALRIGHT THERE WAS NOTHING BUT A LOAD OF STUFF CAME AFTERWARDS. I
THINK THAT REALLY AFFECTED MY VIEW ON IT BECAUSE I FELT WHAT IS
THERE BEYOND LIFE, THAT SPECIFIC PART OF ME SEEING THE PERCEIVED
SENSE OF DEATH. IT FELT LIKE AT RANDOM I WENT BACK INTO THE
REINCARNATION I WAS IN, BUT BY CHANCE I COULD EASILY COME BACK AS
SOMETHING ELSE. SO, THAT WAS THE BIGGEST THING THAT INFLUENCED ME,
FEELING THE PRESENCE OF OTHERS AFTER DEATH.

RB: IN THAT PRESENCE DID YOU FEEL SOMETHING GREATER, SOMETHING
DIVINE OR A GREATER ENTITY?

P: YES I CERTAINLY DID BUT I FELT THAT WAS MYSELF, THE ENTITY I WAS IN
CONTROL OF ALTHOUGH I DIDN’T FEEL MUCH CONTROL IN THE FIRST
EXPERIENCE AND THE ENTITIES ALL AROUND ME WERE ALL CONTROLLED BY
THE SAME INTELLIGENCE AND ALIEN GHOST LIKE FELT VERY DIVINE, LIKE
THOUSANDS OF THEM, THEY WERE ALL TELEPATHICALLY LINKED AND ON
THE SAME PAGE, THEY WERE ALL GODLIKE.

RB: SO THEY WERE ALL INTERCONNECTED THESE FEELINGS AND THINGS?

P: YES.

RB: DID THAT EXPERIENCE CHANGE YOU VIEW OF DEATH AT ALL?

P: I THINK SO, I WOULD SAY THE EXPERIENCE OF THE ENTITIES MADE ME
FEEL LIKE THERE IS LIFE OUT THERE IN ANOTHER DIMENSION AND THAT WE
CAN INTERACT WITH IT, IT HAS MADE ME FEEL CALMER ABOUT DEATH AND
DYING.

RB: WITH THE OUT OF BODY EXPERIENCE HAS IT EXPANDED YOUR VIEW OF
DEATH?

P: YES ON A PHYSICAL LEVEL, BUT IF I WAS ON A TALL BUILDING, THE FEAR
OF THE HEIGHT BUT ON A CONCEPTUAL LEVEL I HAVEN’T GOT THE FEAR OF
DEATH AFTER THAT BUT IF I WAS ON A LEDGE OF A BUILDING I WOULD HAVE
A FEAR BUT I DON’T HAVE A FEAR OF DEATH, BECAUSE THERE IS SOMETHING
AFTER BUT IF THERE ISN’T FOR SURE AFTER IT I KNOW WHAT I HAVE
GLEANED IT’S OK, IT’S JUST THE NEXT STAGE. THE OUT-OF-BODY ASPECT
SHOWS THERE IS SO MUCH MORE TO REALITY AND EXPERIENCES THAT WE
DON’T KNOW OR PERCEIVE. JUST THE AWARENESS THAT EXISTS OF BEING
ABLE TO SEE MY BODY FROM OUTSIDE JUST SHOWS THAT THE PHYSICAL
BODY AND THE SPIRIT AND THE SOUL ARE NOT INTRINSICALLY LINKED THEY
CAN BE VERY MUCH SEPARATE AND CAN GO BACK TOGETHER AND IT
DOESN’T FEEL IMPORTANT TO THE PHYSICAL BODY IT’S ONLY TEMPORARY.

RB: CAN YOU CLARIFY THAT SPECIFIC THING ABOUT THE SOUL LEAVING THE
BODY POTENTIALLY SURVIVING THE DEATH OF THE PHYSICAL BODY, WAS
THAT AN UNDERSTANDING OR A BELIEF HAS SPECIFICALLY BEEN
IMPLEMENTED BY THE OUT OF BODY AND AYAHUASCA EXPERIENCE OR WAS
THAT SOMETHING YOU HAD REAFFIRMED?

P: THIS PART OF IT IS SOMETHING I HAVE BEEN QUESTIONING FOR SOME
TIME SINCE THE LAST EXPERIENCE. THAT’S HARD TO SAY BUT I HAVE DONE A
LOT OF RESEARCH ON IT MYSELF. I HAVE HEARD A LOT OF PEOPLE TALKING
ABOUT IT AND MAYBE IT’S JUST A SENSE OF GOING INTO IT WITH
EXPECTATIONS AND THOSE EXPECTATIONS JUST MANIFESTING FOR ME
BECAUSE I WANTED TO SEE AND I WENT INTO IT WITH AN OPEN MIND OR
IT’S JUST A CASE THAT DIFFERENT PEOPLE SEE DIFFERENT THINGS. SOME OF
THE STUFF I HAD HEARD ABOUT I DEFINITELY DIDN’T EXPERIENCE. BUT I DID
EXPERIENCE SOME THINGS THAT I HADN’T HEARD OF, SO SUBJECTIVELY IT’S
IMPOSSIBLE TO MAKE THAT DISCERNMENT. SORRY, WHAT WAS THE
QUESTION?

RB: DO YOU FEEL THE OUT OF BODY PROCESS AND INSTILLING AND RELATING
TO YOU HAVING AN UNDERSTANDING THAT THE SOUL CAN LEAVE THE BODY
AND TRANSCENDING AND SOMETIMES COMING IN. WAS THAT REAFFIRMED

OR WAS THAT SOMETHING THAT AROSE FROM THE EXPERIENCE?

P: I FEEL LIKE I WAS OPEN TO THE CASE, I DON’T KNOW IF I NECESSARILY
BELIEVED IN IT. IF SOMEBODY PRESSED ME I PROBABLY WOULD SAY YES. NOT
IN A SENSE I WAS COMFORTABLE IN IT, ZERO CONFIDENCE IN IT, BUT AT A
GUESS THAT’S ME. AFTER IT I FEEL MUCH MORE COMFORTABLE IN IT, STILL
NOT A HUNDRED PERCENT IN IT, IT COULD ALL HAVE BEEN A
HALLUCINATION, BUT IT DEFINITELY FELT VERY REAL. SO IT WASN’T THE
AYAHUASCA THAT STARTED THE IDEA, IN A VARIETY OF OTHER PRINCIPLES
AND TEXTS AND DIFFERENT IDEAS. I WAS INCLINED TO BELIEVE IT. BUT IT
COULD BE THE AYAHUASCA THAT CONFIRMED IT. THE EXPERIENCE MADE IT
FEEL MUCH MORE REAL. I DON’T KNOW IF YOU CAN TRUST YOUR
EXPERIENCES OR WHAT SOMEONE ELSE IS SAYING.

RB: GOOD ANSWER. MOVING ON TO THE NEXT QUESTION. HAS THE
EXPERIENCE EXPANDED YOUR SENSE OF YOUR BODY, YOU HAVE TOUCHED ON
THIS BEFORE IN DIFFERENT WAYS, THAT THERE WAS A REDUCTION IN THE
FEAR OF DEATH, YOU TALKED ABOUT SEEING YOUR CONSCIOUSNESS AND
YOUR BODY AS A SEPARATE ENTITY, IS THERE ANY OTHER WAY THAT THINGS
EXPANDED YOUR VIEW OR RELATIONSHIP TO YOUR PHYSICAL BODY, DO YOU
FEEL LESS CONNECTED TO IT OR MORE APPRECIATE OF IT OR LESS. YOU SAID
IN THE EXPERIENCE A LOT OF THINGS SEEMED LESS IMPORTANT AND THINGS
THAT STAYED WITH YOU?

P: IT’S LIKE A PARADOX OR A CONTRADICTION, MY THINGS OF MY INDIVIDUAL
SELF AND MY BODY FEEL LESS SIGNIFICANT THAT ISN’T IN A SENSE THAT’S
IT’S WORTH NEGLECTING. IT’S LIKE THE OPPOSITE, IT’S GOING TO BE GONE SO
MAKE THE MOST OF IT. ALL THERE IS TO IT IS TO LIVE WELL AND THAT LOVE
IS THE KEY FOCUS. KINDNESS TOWARDS OTHERS AND YOURSELF SHOULD BE
THE PRIMARY FOCUS AT ANY TIME, IN THAT BECOMES SELF LOVE AND
EATING HEALTHILY. IT JUST PUTS STUFF INTO PERSPECTIVE. I WOULDN’T SAY
I FEEL LESS CONNECTED TO MY PHYSICAL BODY, THERE IS A LOT MORE TO IT
THAN IT. IT’S LIKE YOU HAVE ONE CAR AND YOU BUY SIX CARS AND DRIVE
THEM ALL EQUALLY. THERE ARE JUST MORE OPTIONS.

RB: AND HAS THE EXPERIENCE EXPANDED YOUR VIEW OF OTHER PEOPLE?

P: YES, IT DEFINITELY HAS, IN PARTICULAR THE DISSOCIATION FROM SELF, IT
HAS INCREASED MY EMPATHY. IT’S MADE ME THINK THAT WHEN PEOPLE
ARE ACTING IN ANY WAY OTHER THAN PLEASANT, BUT JUST KNOW THAT
WHATEVER THEIR PERSPECTIVE IS, THEY HAVE REACHED THAT THROUGH
THEIR INDIVIDUAL EXPERIENCE AND EVERYONE IS DOING THEIR BEST NO
MATTER HOW THEY ARE DOING THEIR OWN THING ON THE INFORMATION
THEY HAVE. I THINK THAT IS ABSOLUTELY THE CASE AND IT OPENS UP A CAN
OF WORMS, POLITICAL VIEWS AND ALL THE THINGS THAT I HAVE THOUGHT,
WORLDLY THINGS, LIKE PRISON THINGS. I’M JUST AS LIKELY TO THINK THAT
THEY DESERVE ANY KIND OF PUNISHMENT. I’M NOT SAYING I BELIEVE IN
PRISON OR NO PRISON BUT FOR EXAMPLE I’M INCLINED TO HAVE A VIEW
BECAUSE WHEN YOUR EMPATHY INCREASES IT MAKES IT EASIER TO SEE

390

THINGS FROM BOTH SIDES. A LOT OF THINGS I HAD FIRM VIEWS ON ARE LESS
FIRM NOW, IN TERMS OF WORLDLY THINGS, LIKE POLITICAL TOPICS. JUST IN
THE WAY OF FEELING I FELT ANGRY WITH PEOPLE SINCE, I HAVE NOT HAD A
PERSONALITY CHANGE LONG TERM BUT JUST A SENSE OF EMPATHY. PEOPLE
ARE NOT AS IMPORTANT AS THEY SEEM, SO IF SOMEBODY DIES IN A SENSE I
AM LESS CONCERNED, I HAVE NOT HAD ANY MAJOR FAMILY DEATHS SINCE
THE EXPERIENCE I’M NOT SURE HOW IT IS GOING TO IMPACT THAT BUT I DO
FEEL MORE PREPARED FOR IT, AND I’M GOING TO HAVE A NATURAL GRIEVING
BUT IT’S NOT GOING TO LINGER AND BE TOXICALLY BAD AS IT WOULD HAVE.

RB: CAN YOU IDENTIFY ANYTHING SPECIFICALLY ABOUT THE AYAHUASCA
EXPERIENCE HAS LED TO THAT FEELING OF GREATER EMPATHY?

P: I THINK IT IS JUST THE ENTITIES THAT WERE SHOWING ME ALL THIS
STUFF, BUT I FELT I CREPT IN THROUGH THE BACK DOOR, I DIDN’T MEAN TO
CREEP IN IT JUST HAPPENED, I JUST APPEARED THERE IN THE MIDDLE OF A
STAGE, I FELT I HAD GONE TOO FAR AND THE ONLY WAY TO GET ME BACK
WAS TO THROW ME BACK THROUGH THE MIDDLE AND SHOW ME
EVERYTHING. THEY WERE TRYING TO LIMIT EVERYTHING I COULD SEE, SO I
COULDN’T SEE EVERYTHING, SO EVERYTHING THAT I SAW INFINITE PEOPLE,
THEY WERE ALL DOING THEIR OWN THING, THEY WERE ALL LIVING THEIR
OWN LIVES AND DIFFERENT ENTITIES DOING THEIR OWN THING AND
THOUGHTS AND PERSPECTIVES AND THERE WERE SO MANY OF THEM, AND IT
WAS LIKE ONE SYMPATHY AND TWO EMPATHY. IT FEELS LIKE A
CONTRADICTION BECAUSE IF YOU FELT MORE EMPATHY TO SOMEONE IT
WOULD BE MORE IMPORTANT BUT IT WASN’T, IT WAS THE SAME THING. YOU
ARE ONLY HURTING YOURSELF IF YOU ARE ACTING NEGATIVELY TOWARDS
SOMEONE BECAUSE THEY ARE YOU. I DO ALSO FEEL LIKE COMING OUT OF MY
BODY MADE ME MORE EMPATHIC AND IN TURN VIEW MYSELF DIFFERENTLY.
IT SHOWED ME I WAS NOT JUST FLESH AND BONE, I’M A CREATURE OF
FEELING AND BEING MORE IN TOUCH WITH OTHER PEOPLE’S FEELINGS
MAKES YOU SEE YOURSELF AS FUNDAMENTALLY THE SAME AS THEM.

RB: GOOD STUFF. HAS YOUR EXPERIENCE EXPANDED YOUR VIEW TO NATURE?

P: YES DEFINITELY, IT’S MADE ME APPRECIATE MUCH MORE, A CLEAR
DIFFERENCE.

RB: CAN YOU IDENTIFY SOMETHING SPECIFICALLY, WAS THERE ANY
INTERCONNECTEDNESS WITH SOMETHING. NOT JUST WITH HUMAN LIFE BUT
WITH OTHER LIFE, DID YOU FEEL CONNECTED TO NATURE?

P: WHEN I TALK ABOUT THESE OTHER PEOPLE I FEEL I’M TALKING ABOUT
TREES, GRASSES, WAVES AND SAND, BEFORE I CAME TO THE AYAHUASCA I
DIDN’T LIKE SAND, BUT I LIKE SAND NOW. IT’S DIFFICULT TO PINPOINT THE
AYAHUASCA BECAUSE MY WHOLE TIME IN PERU, BACK PACKING HAS
CHANGED THIS. IN THE RETREAT CENTRE THERE WERE HAMMOCKS AND
GRASS AND MY SENSE PERCEPTIONS WERE MASSIVELY INCREASED, SO
FEELING TEXTURES AND STONES ON THE FLOOR AND THERE WERE DOGS

NATURE & IMPACT OF OUT-OF-BODY EXPERIENCES

523

WHICH I HAD A REALLY DEEP CONNECTION WITH, AND ON MY FINAL TIME I
WAS WALKING AROUND WITH THIS BIG LABRADOR WHICH WAS HUGE AND
EVERYONE LOVED HIM, I ENDED UP LYING ON THE FLOOR WITH HIM, SPENT
FOUR OR FIVE HOURS SLEEPING WITH HIM AND JUST WALKING AROUND THE
AREA ON THE FINAL TIME AT NIGHT AND IT WAS QUITE COLD AND I WAS
ENJOYING IT. WALKING WITH A BLANKET AROUND ME PAST THE TREES,
SITTING IN THE HAMMOCK AND YOU DO THE THING WHERE YOU DON’T EAT
FOR CERTAIN DAYS, IT MAKES YOUR HUNGER GO UP AND MY APPRECIATION
FOR FRUIT REALLY WENT UP AND AN APPLE WAS THE FIRST THING I BIT
INTO AFTER MY FIRST AYAHUASCA AND IT TASTED COMPLETELY DIFFERENT
TO WHAT I HAVE TASTED BEFORE, INSANELY DIFFERENT. IT WAS ONLY
AFTER THE AYAHUASCA THAT I WAS ONLY TRULY ABLE TO TASTE APPLE,
BREAD AND SOUP AND THINGS LIKE THAT. THEY HAD ALL SORTS OF
PERUVIAN FRUIT, THINGS I HADN’T TASTED BEFORE. I GUESS MY EXPOSURE
WHILST UNDER THE INFLUENCE OF AYAHUASCA JUST REMINDED ME OF
THINGS I HAD ALREADY KNOWN AND FORGOTTEN. LIVING IN A CITY ALL MY
LIFE. DURING THE AYAHUASCA I DIDN’T THINK AT ANY STAGE THAT THIS
WAS EXCLUSIVE, I JUST FELT THAT THIS WAS PART OF IT, THERE WAS A
POINT OUT OF MY BODY WHERE I WAS NOT ME ANYMORE AND THERE WAS
JUST THIS FEELING OF INTERCONNECTEDNESS WITH EVERYTHING, IT WAS
LIKE NATURE INCLUDES EVERYTHING. NATURE INCLUDES A BIG FACTORY
THAT IS POLLUTING THE WORLD, IT WAS MADE BY HUMANS OUT OF STUFF IN
A SENSE THAT EVERYTHING IS NATURAL, THE ORGANIC BECAUSE SOME
THINGS ARE MANMADE BECAUSE EVERYTHING THAT HAPPENS IS NATURAL.
NATURE JUST MEANS WHAT IS, IN A WAY IT JUST CHANGED MY VIEW OF
WHAT NATURE IS.IT HAS ALSO MADE ME LIVE A LESS MATERIALISTIC LIFE, IM
MORE UNDERSTANDING AND LESS SELF CENTRED, I'M MORE CAPABLE OF
LETTING THINGS GO.

RB: CAN YOU IDENTIFY ANY NEGATIVE EXPERIENCES OUT OF THE
EXPERIENCE?

P: ONLY THAT I WANT TO GO BACK AND DO IT ALL AGAIN. I GIVE MYSELF A
FIVE YEAR MINIMUM, I DON’T KNOW WHAT IS GOING TO HAPPEN TO ALLOW
ME OR NOT ALLOW ME TO DO IT AGAIN. AT LEAST ONCE A MONTH I WILL
THINK ABOUT IT WHY I WANT TO GO BACK AND REACH THAT STATE AGAIN.
JUST A LONGING BECAUSE I FEEL AT HOME THERE, AT PEACE AND AWAY
FROM STRESS WHERE IT’S SO IMPORTANT TO HAVE YOUR WORK DONE ON
TIME. THERE WERE MOMENTS IN IT WHERE IT FELT SCARY BUT AT NO TIME
DID I FEEL IT WASN’T A GOOD EXPERIENCE AFTER ALL. I DON’T FEEL IT HAS
LED TO ANYTHING NEGATIVE LONG TERM IN MY LIFE. THE EFFECT OF THE
AYAHUASCA HAS IMPROVED ME IN MANY WAYS BUT IT HASN’T MADE ME
PERFECT LIKE JESUS, BUT IT DIDN’T REACH THAT FAR WHICH I AM NOT
SURPRISED ABOUT IN THE THREE TIMES AND I FEEL THERE IS A LOT MORE
WORK TO BE DONE.

RB: CAN YOU IDENTIFY ANY OTHER POSITIVE EXPERIENCES THAT WE HAVE
NOT TALKED ABOUT?

P: I FEEL USING THE WORD INSIGNIFICANT ABOUT LIFE, THE CONNOTATIONS
MAKES IT FEEL IT’S INFERIOR IF YOU DIDN’T SAY IT WAS INSIGNIFICANT. IT
DOESN’T MEAN YOU SHOULDN’T CARE, IT IS A FINE LINE AND
PARADOXICALLY IT’S MADE ME FEEL IT’S NOT AS SIGNIFICANT AS PEOPLE
JUDGE IT TO BE. WHERE THERE IS NOTHING FOR ME TO DO AND I’M NOT
WITH PEOPLE WHO ARE VERY INTERESTING, THE EMPATHY HELPS WITH
THAT AND IF I’M IN A HOSTILE POSITION THE EMPATHY HELPS. THE SENSE OF
EVERYTHING BEING LESS IMPORTANT THAN WE NEED AND IN MANAGEMENT
TIME I DON’T WANT TO BE DOING ANYTHING THAT IS NOT IMPORTANT TO
ME. I FEEL THAT IS MUCH LESS OF A STRESS ON ME, I CAN BE IN AN
ENVIRONMENT THAT I DON’T FEEL VERY HAPPY IN AND DOESN’T STIMULATE
ME I FEEL THAT’S FINE AND IT DOESN’T MATTER, IN THE GRAND SCHEME OF
THINGS IT’S NOT IMPORTANT BUT IT COULD LEAD TO A NIHILISTIC OUTLOOK
ON LIFE BUT IN MY CASE IT ALLOW ME TO BE A BIT MORE NEUTRAL IN
SITUATIONS WHERE I WOULD NORMALLY BE GETTING CAUGHT UP IN THE
ATMOSPHERE. LIKE IF EVERYBODY IS STRESSED OUT I CAN JUST SIT THERE
AND DRINK TEA, IT DOESN’T MEAN I’M AWAY WITH THE FAIRIES AND READY
TO STEP INTO ACTION IF IT IS REQUIRED I WOULD BE STRAIGHT ON IT, BUT IN
MOMENTS WHEN IT IS CALM AND I DON’T NEED TO DO ANYTHING I CAN
HAPPILY DO THAT, MUCH EASIER THAN BEFORE.

RB: IS THERE ANYTHING IMPORTANT THAT WE HAVE NOT DISCUSSED OR
THAT YOU WOULD LIKE TO SHARE?

P: THERE ARE LOTS OF THINGS WE HAVEN’T GONE INTO AND I DID WRITE
NOTES, BUT I FEEL A LOT OF THE EXPERIENCES I HAD WERE TOO MUCH FOR
MY MIND. NOT TOO MUCH AT THE TIME BUT TOO MUCH FOR ME TO
COMPARTMENTALISE. THERE ARE BLANKS AND BLURS IT WAS LIKE A SUPER
HIGH VISION BUT MY MIND ONLY RECALLS A SMALL AMOUNT. IT WAS VERY
HARD TO TELL WHAT WAS REAL AND WHAT WASN’T. I FEEL LIKE
EVERYTHING I SAW AND THINK SHOULD BE TAKEN WITH A PINCH OF SALT,
SUCH SUBJECTIVE STUFF AND THAT’S WHY I FIND IT INTERESTING TO LOOK
AT PATTERNS AND DIFFERENT PEOPLE’S EXPERIENCE THAT’S CONSTANT BUT
I WITNESSED TESTIMONY SO THERE WAS DEFINITELY A LOT MORE IT WAS
LIKE A FLAVOUR OF THE 3 EXPERIENCES, THE FIRST ONE FELT LIKE AN
EXPLOSION. I DID MENTION THE DOSES, THE FIRST TIME I HAD A VERY HIGH
DOSE, THE SECOND TIME THEY HALVED THE DOSE AND THE THIRD TIME
THEY PUT IT HIGHER THAN THE FIRST ONE. BUT I FELT THAT BY THE THIRD
TIME I HAD THE ABILITY TO HANDLE IT AND MASTER IT AND HAVE CONTROL
OF THE EXPERIENCE AND I FELT VERY MUCH IN CONTROL IN THAT STATE OF
AWARENESS AND CONSCIOUSNESS BUT CONTROL WAS GOING ON, IT WAS
COMFORTABLE. THE FIRST TIME I FELT I WAS THROWN IN AT THE DEEP END,
IT WAS JUST LIKE CRAZY AND I ENDED UP HAVING THAT SEIZURE AND
EVERYONE WAS CONCERNED ABOUT ME, BUT I WAS FINE. THE SECOND TIME
DUE TO THAT THEY HALVED THE DOSE AND TOLD ME HOW TO HOLD
CONTROL AND IT WAS LIKE LEARNING HOW TO SWIM AND I FELT IN LONG
TERM PSYCHOLOGICAL EFFECT THERE WAS THE MOST EXPERIENCE THERE,
THAT ONE HAD THE LEAST HALLUCINOGENIC EFFECTS IT WAS DEFINITELY A
DEEP SENSE OF EFFECTIVENESS AND A LOT OF WORK WENT ON IN THAT

SECOND ONE AND I FELT I DEALT WITH A LOT OF PSYCHOLOGICAL
COMPLEXES THAT I HAVE. I WAS ABLE TO HEAL IN THE SECOND ONE AND I
FELT THAT WAS MASSIVELY BENEFICIAL AND I REALLY DID WELL IN THAT
ONE AND THE LAST ONE I FELT I WAS A MASTER AT THAT STAGE AND I WAS
ABLE TO DRINK A LOT MORE AND HAVE A LOT OF EXPERIENCES AND HAVE A
LOT OF EXPERIENCES LIKE THE FIRST TIME BUT NOT BEING THROWN INTO
THE THING AND FEELING MY ARMS WERE TIED, I ALSO HAD CONTROL OVER
MY PHYSICAL BODY AND I WAS ABLE TO WALK ABOUT IN THE PLACE AND I
DIDN’T EVEN SLEEP THE WHOLE NIGHT OR PURGING OR VOMITING THE
THIRD TIME, I JUST KEPT IT IN AND STAYED AWAKE AND FELT FINE THE
NEXT DAY. IT STAYED IN ME AND I WAS ABLE TO MANIPULATE MY REALITY. I
FELT SENSATIONS OF FLYING AND BEING ABLE TO LEVITATE BUT THAT WAS
AT A TIME WHEN EVERYONE HAD GONE TO SLEEP AND I WAS BY MYSELF. I
COULDN’T ASK ANYONE IF I WAS ACTUALLY FLYING, YES THERE WAS LOTS OF
STUFF.

RB: WERE THOSE SENSATIONS DURING THE LAST CEREMONY?

P: YES, DURING THE FINAL CEREMONY WHILE IT WAS AFTER THE CEREMONY,
BUT I FELT THAT BECAUSE I HADN’T BEEN SICK THE SENSATIONS WERE
GOING TO CARRY ON. THEY SAID YOU WERE WELCOME TO STAY ON BUT THEY
WERE GOING TO BED. THEY DID BLOOD TESTS ON ME AND THEY WERE
NORMAL. EVERYTHING WAS NORMAL BUT I WAS STILL IN MY HEAD AND IT
WAS CRAZY. AT MOMENTS IT FELT LIKE MY BODY WAS BEING PULLED, I
COULD CHOOSE TO RESIST IT OR JUST STAY FOR LONGER AND JUST DO WHAT
IT WAS MAKING ME DO. MAKING ME GO AND DO DIFFERENT THINGS AND SAY
THINGS TO DIFFERENT PEOPLE, BECAUSE I MADE LOTS OF FRIENDS OVER
THERE, GO TO GET A PIECE OF BREAD OR STAND ON ONE LEG, I FELT I WAS
JUST GOING ALONG WITH IT AND A LOT OF LAUGHTER. I WAS HAPPY AND
CONTENT AND IT FELT LIKE A GOOD ENDING AND CLOSURE, BUT IT
DEFINITELY FELT THAT THERE WAS MORE AND IT REALLY STUCK WITH ME
WHAT THEY WERE SAYING THAT HE IS NOT READY FOR THIS YET OR JUST
DOESN’T NEED TO BE HERE YET, IT WAS ALMOST LIKE A SENSE I DIDN’T HAVE
ENOUGH DAMAGE THAT NEEDED HEALING. I FELT I WENT INTO IT VERY OPEN
MINDED AND I WAS IN A VERY GOOD PLACE AT THAT TIME. IT WAS WHEN I
TURNED EIGHTEEN THAT I WAS GOING TO DO BACK PACKING AND BUNGEE
JUMPING, AND I JUST WENT INTO IT AND FELT HAPPY. I DIDN’T HAVE A LOT
THAT NEEDED HEALING AND I NEEDED TO GO BACK LATER. I WOULD GO
BACK TO IT I DON’T KNOW IF IT WILL BE YEARS OR DECADES.

528

END RECORDING
